# Tuya Smart Home iOS SDK - Binaries (arm64 Simulator Support)

This repository contains the actual XCFramework binaries for Tuya Smart Home iOS SDK with arm64 simulator support.

## Important Notes

- ⚠️ **DO NOT clone this repository** - binaries are distributed via GitHub Releases
- ✅ Use CocoaPods or Swift Package Manager for installation
- 📦 Each framework has its own release tag and downloadable ZIP

## Installation

### CocoaPods

```ruby
source 'https://github.com/programming086/TuyaSimulatorFixed-Specs.git'
source 'https://github.com/CocoaPods/Specs.git'

platform :ios, '11.0'

target 'YourApp' do
  use_frameworks!
  pod 'TuyaSmartActivatorKit'
end
```

### Swift Package Manager

In Xcode: File → Add Packages → 
`https://github.com/programming086/TuyaSimulatorFixed-SPM.git`
